(herald "Session Binding Protocol (SBP)")

(comment "CPSA 3.6.6")

(comment "All input read from sbp.lsp")

(defprotocol sbp basic
  (defrole client
    (vars (request request2 answer answer2 cookie data)
      (client proxy name))
    (trace (init request)
      (recv (enc "resp" answer cookie (privk proxy)))
      (send (enc "req" request2 cookie (privk client)))
      (recv (enc "resp2" answer2 cookie (privk proxy)))))
  (defrole proxy
    (vars (request2 answer answer2 cookie data) (client proxy name))
    (trace (obsv (cat answer cookie))
      (send (enc "resp" answer cookie (privk proxy)))
      (recv (enc "req" request2 cookie (privk client)))
      (init (cat request2 cookie)) (obsv (cat answer2 cookie))
      (send (enc "resp2" answer2 cookie (privk proxy)))))
  (defrole server
    (vars (request request2 answer answer2 cookie data))
    (trace (tran request (cat answer cookie))
      (tran (cat request2 cookie) answer2))))

(defskeleton sbp
  (vars (request request2 answer answer2 cookie data)
    (client proxy name))
  (defstrand client 4 (request request) (request2 request2)
    (answer answer) (answer2 answer2) (cookie cookie) (client client)
    (proxy proxy))
  (non-orig (privk client) (privk proxy))
  (traces
    ((init request) (recv (enc "resp" answer cookie (privk proxy)))
      (send (enc "req" request2 cookie (privk client)))
      (recv (enc "resp2" answer2 cookie (privk proxy)))))
  (label 0)
  (unrealized (0 1) (0 3))
  (origs)
  (comment "1 in cohort - 1 not yet seen"))

(defskeleton sbp
  (vars (request request2 request2-0 answer cookie data)
    (client proxy client-0 name))
  (defstrand client 4 (request request) (request2 request2)
    (answer answer) (answer2 request2-0) (cookie cookie) (client client)
    (proxy proxy))
  (defstrand server 1 (request request) (answer answer) (cookie cookie))
  (defstrand proxy 6 (request2 request2-0) (answer answer)
    (answer2 request2-0) (cookie cookie) (client client-0)
    (proxy proxy))
  (precedes ((0 0) (1 0)) ((1 0) (2 0)) ((2 1) (0 1)) ((2 5) (0 3)))
  (leadsto ((0 0) (1 0)) ((1 0) (2 0)) ((2 3) (2 4)))
  (non-orig (privk client) (privk proxy))
  (operation state-passing-test (displaced 3 2 proxy 4)
    (cat request2-1 cookie) (2 4))
  (traces
    ((init request) (recv (enc "resp" answer cookie (privk proxy)))
      (send (enc "req" request2 cookie (privk client)))
      (recv (enc "resp2" request2-0 cookie (privk proxy))))
    ((tran request (cat answer cookie)))
    ((obsv (cat answer cookie))
      (send (enc "resp" answer cookie (privk proxy)))
      (recv (enc "req" request2-0 cookie (privk client-0)))
      (init (cat request2-0 cookie)) (obsv (cat request2-0 cookie))
      (send (enc "resp2" request2-0 cookie (privk proxy)))))
  (label 35)
  (parent 0)
  (unrealized)
  (shape)
  (maps
    ((0)
      ((client client) (proxy proxy) (request request)
        (request2 request2) (answer answer) (answer2 request2-0)
        (cookie cookie))))
  (origs))
